üîπ 6. –ê–Ω–∞–ª–∏—Ç–∏–∫–∞ –∏ –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç—ã - –¢–û–ü-15 –Ω–µ–π—Ä–æ—Å–µ—Ç–µ–π –∏ –ò–ò –¥–ª—è –Ω–∞–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–∏—è –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç–æ–≤ –ø–æ –ø—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–∏–∫–µ –≤ 2025 –≥–æ–¥—É ‚Äî –ù–∏–∫–∏—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ vc.ru ‚Äì –∏–∑—É—á–∏ –≤–æ–∑—å–º–∏ –ª—É—á—à–µ–µ

–í —Ä–∞–∑–µ–¥–ª–µ –∫–ª–∏–Ω–∏–Ω–≥ —É–±–æ—Ä–∫–∞ –ø–æ–¥—ä–¥–æ–≤ –º—ã –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω—ã –≤–∏–¥–∏—Ç—å –∫–∞–∂–¥–æ—ã–π —Ä–∞–±–æ—á–∏–π –¥–µ–Ω—å –≤ —Ä–µ–∂–∏–º–µ –æ–Ω–ª–∞–π–Ω —Å–æ –≤—Å–µ–º–∏ –º–∞—Ä—à—Ä—É—Ç–∞–º–∏ –ø–µ—Ä–≤–∏–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∑–∞—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–∏ –∏ —Ç–¥ –∏ —Ç–ø 
 —Ä–∞–∑–¥–µ–ª -—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–π–∫–∞  –≤–æ—Ä–æ–Ω–∫–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–¥–∞–∂ ‚Äì –≤–∑—è—Ç—å –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –æ—Ç—Ç—É–¥–∞ / –¥–∞—Ç—å –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –±—Ä–∞—Ç—å –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –∏–∑ —Ü—Ä–º ‚Äì –∏ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—å –≤ –¥–∞—à –±–æ—Ä–¥–µ ‚Äì –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è—Ç—å –≤ —Ü—Ä–º –≤ –Ω—É–∂–Ω—É—é –≤–æ—Ä–æ–Ω–∫—É –Ω–æ–≤—ã–π –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑, –ø—Ä–æ—â–µ –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –µ–∂–µ–¥–Ω–µ–≤–Ω–∞—è –ø–æ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–º –∏ —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∏ –≤–µ—Å—Ç–∏ —É—á–µ—Ç –¥–ª—è –∫–∞–∂–¥–æ–≥–æ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑—É –≤ –¥–∞—à –±–æ—Ä–¥–µ –ø–æ –∑–∞—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç –º–∞—Ç–µ—Ä–∏–ª–∞ –¥–µ–Ω—å–≥–∏–º –∏ —Ç–¥
8)	–§–∏–Ω–∞–Ω—Å—ã ‚Äì –≤ —Ä–∞–∑–¥–µ–ª–µ —Ñ–∏–Ω–∞–Ω—Å—ã —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å –ø–æ–ª–Ω–æ—Ü–µ–Ω–Ω—É—é —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω—á–µ—Å–∫—É—é –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –ø–æ –≤–∫–ª–∞–¥–∫–∞–º, –≤ –î–î–° —Ñ–∞–∫—Ç / –ø–ª–∞–Ω ‚Äì —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞–π —á—Ç–æ–± –º—ã –º–æ–≥–ª–∏ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—è—Ç—å —É–±–∏—Ä–∞—Ç—å —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—å–∏ –∏ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª—è—Ç—å —Ñ–∏–Ω–∞–Ω—Å–æ–≤—ã–π –ø–ª–∞–Ω –∏ —Å–≤–æ–¥–Ω–æ–π –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å—é —Å–æ–æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ, —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞–π –∫–∞–∫ –≥–µ–Ω–∏–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π —Ñ–∏–Ω–Ω–∞—Å–∏—Å—Ç/—Ä–∞–∑—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—á–∏–∫

üîπ 1. CRM –∏ –î–æ–≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä—ã
–¢—ã –¥–æ–ª–∂–µ–Ω –±—ã—Ç—å –∏–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω

‚Ä¢	–°–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è —Å Bitrix24 (—Å–¥–µ–ª–∫–∏, –∑–∞–¥–∞—á–∏, –∑–≤–æ–Ω–∫–∏, –¥–∏—Å–∫, –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª–∏,).

üîπ 2. –ü–ª–∞–Ω–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç

üîπ 4. –ó–≤–æ–Ω–∫–∏
–ë–æ—Ç –¥–æ–ª–∂–µ–Ω –∏–º–µ—Ç—å –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å —Å–æ–≤–µ—Ä—à–∞—Ç—å –∏—Å—Ö–æ–¥—è—â–∏–µ –∑–≤–æ–Ω–∫–∏ –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–º —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ –±–∏—Ç—Ä–∏–∫—Å24 –Ω–æ–≤–æ—Ñ–æ–Ω —Å –æ–ø–æ–≤–µ—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ–º –ø–æ–∑–¥—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ–º —Ñ–∏–¥ –±–µ–∫–æ–º –∏ —Ç–¥ –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–º–µ—Ä –£ –≤–∞—Å –µ—Å—Ç—å –Ω–∞—Ä–µ–∫–∞–Ω–∏–µ –∫ –∫–∞—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤—É —É–±–æ—Ä–∫–∏ ? –ù–µ—Ç ‚Äì –æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç  –æ—Ç–ª–∏—á–Ω–æ, —Ç–æ–≥–¥–∞ –æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤—å—Ç–µ –æ—Ç–∑—ã–≤ —è –≤–∞–º –ø—Ä–∏—à–ª—é —Å—Å—ã–ª–∫—É –≤ —Ç–µ–ª–µ–≥—Ä–∞–º –±—É–¥–µ–º –≤–∞–º –æ—á–µ–Ω—å –±–ª–∞–≥–æ–¥—Ä–Ω—ã –Ω–∞—à–∏–º —Å–æ—Ç—Ä—É–¥–Ω–∏–∫–∞–º –≤—Å–µ–≥–¥–∞ –ø—Ä–∏—è—Ç–Ω–æ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∞—Ç—å –æ–±—Ä–∞—Ç–Ω—É—é —Å–≤—è–∑—å –æ—Ç –∂–∏—Ç–µ–ª–µ–π –º–Ω–æ–≥–æ–∫–≤–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä–Ω—ã–∑—Ö –¥–æ–º–æ–≤ —Å—Å—ã–ª–∫–∏ –∫—É–¥–∞ 

üîπ 4. –ö–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–æ–ª—å –∫–∞—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–∞
‚Ä¢	AI-–∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑ —Ñ–æ—Ç–æ–æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç–æ–≤ (–æ–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∫–∞—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–∞ —É–±–æ—Ä–∫–∏, –ø—Ä–æ–ø—É—â–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –∑–æ–Ω).

/app/backend/server.py:
1|from fastapi import FastAPI, APIRouter
2|from dotenv import load_dotenv
3|from starlette.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
4|from motor.motor_asyncio import AsyncIOMotorClient
5|import os
6|import logging
7|from pathlib import Path
8|from pydantic import BaseModel, Field
9|from typing import List
10|import uuid
11|from datetime import datetime
12|
13|
14|ROOT_DIR = Path(__file__).parent
15|load_dotenv(ROOT_DIR / '.env')
16|
17|# MongoDB connection
18|mongo_url = os.environ['MONGO_URL']
19|client = AsyncIOMotorClient(mongo_url)
20|db = client[os.environ['DB_NAME']]
21|
22|# Create the main app without a prefix
23|app = FastAPI()
24|
25|# Create a router with the /api prefix
26|api_router = APIRouter(prefix="/api")
27|
28|
29|# Define Models
30|class StatusCheck(BaseModel):
31|    id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))
32|    client_name: str
33|    timestamp: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)
34|
35|class StatusCheckCreate(BaseModel):
36|    client_name: str
37|
38|# Add your routes to the router instead of directly to app
39|@api_router.get("/")
40|async def root():
41|    return {"message": "Hello World"}
42|
43|@api_router.post("/status", response_model=StatusCheck)
44|async def create_status_check(input: StatusCheckCreate):
45|    status_dict = input.dict()
46|    status_obj = StatusCheck(**status_dict)
47|    _ = await db.status_checks.insert_one(status_obj.dict())
48|    return status_obj
49|
50|@api_router.get("/status", response_model=List[StatusCheck])
51|async def get_status_checks():
52|    status_checks = await db.status_checks.find().to_list(1000)
53|    return [StatusCheck(**status_check) for status_check in status_checks]
54|
55|# Include the router in the main app
56|app.include_router(api_router)
57|
58|app.add_middleware(
59|    CORSMiddleware,
60|    allow_credentials=True,
61|    allow_origins=os.environ.get('CORS_ORIGINS', '*').split(','),
62|    allow_methods=["*"],
63|    allow_headers=["*"],
64|)
65|
66|# Configure logging
67|logging.basicConfig(
68|    level=logging.INFO,
69|    format='%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s'
70|)
71|logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
72|
73|@app.on_event("shutdown")
74|async def shutdown_db_client():
75|    client.close()
76|

Optional[str] = None, end_date: Optional[str] = None):\n    """–§–∏–Ω–∞–Ω—Å–æ–≤—ã–π –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç"""\n    try:\n        # –£—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞–≤–ª–∏–≤–∞–µ–º –¥–∏–∞–ø–∞–∑–æ–Ω –¥–∞—Ç (–ø–æ —É–º–æ–ª—á–∞–Ω–∏—é —Ç–µ–∫—É—â–∏–π –º–µ—Å—è—Ü)\n        if not start_date:\n            start = datetime.utcnow().replace(day=1, hour=0, minute=0, second=0, microsecond=0)\n        else:\n            start = datetime.fromisoformat(start_date)\n            \n        if not end_date:\n            end = datetime.utcnow()\n        else:\n            end = datetime.fromisoformat(end_date)\n        \n        # –ê–≥—Ä–µ–≥–∞—Ü–∏—è –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö\n        pipeline = [\n            {"$match": {"date": {"$gte": start, "$lte": end}}},\n            {"$group": {\n                "_id": {"category": "$category", "subcategory": "$subcategory"},\n                "total": {"$sum": "$amount"},\n                "count": {"$sum": 1}\n            }},\n            {"$sort": {"total": -1}}\n        ]\n        \n        cursor = db.finance_entries.aggregate(pipeline)\n        results = await cursor.to_list(length=None)\n        \n        # –ì—Ä—É–ø–ø–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –ø–æ –∫–∞—Ç–µ–≥–æ—Ä–∏—è–º\n        report = {"revenue": {}, "expense": {}, "investment": {}}\n        totals = {"revenue": 0, "expense": 0, "investment": 0}\n        \n        for result in results:\n            category = result["_id"]["category"]\n            subcategory = result["_id"]["subcategory"]\n            \n            if category not in report:\n                report[category] = {}\n                \n            report[category][subcategory] = {\n                "amount": result["total"],\n                "count": result["count"]\n            }\n            totals[category] += result["total"]\n        \n        return {\n            "period": {"start": start, "end": end},\n            "totals": totals,\n            "profit": totals["revenue"] - totals["expense"],\n            "breakdown": report\n        }\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))\n\n# ====== AI AND ANALYTICS ======\n\n@api_router.get("/ai/analysis")\nasync def +#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""
+VasDom AI Business Management System - Backend API Testing
+Comprehensive test suite for all backend endpoints
+"""
+
+import requests
+import sys
+import json
+from datetime import datetime
+from typing import Dict, Any, List
+
+class VasDomAPITester:
+    def __init__(self, base_url="https://smart-biz-dash.preview.emergentagent.com"):
+        self.base_url = base_url
+        self.api_url = f"{base_url}/api"
+        self.tests_run = 0
+        self.tests_passed = 0
+        self.failed_tests = []
+
+    def log_test(self, name: str, success: bool, details: str = ""):
+        """Log test results"""
+        self.tests_run += 1
+        status = "‚úÖ PASS" if success else "‚ùå FAIL"
+        print(f"{status} - {name}")
+        if details:
+            print(f"    Details: {details}")
+        
+        if success:
+            self.tests_passed += 1
+        else:
+            self.failed_tests.append({"name": name, "details": details})
+
+    def test_endpoint(self, name: str, method: str, endpoint: str, expected_status: int = 200, data: Dict = None) -> tuple:
+        """Test a single endpoint"""
+        url = f"{self.base_url}/{endpoint}" if not endpoint.startswith('/api') else f"{self.base_url}{endpoint}"
+        headers = {'Content-Type': 'application/json'}
+        
+        try:
+            if method == 'GET':
+                response = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=10)
+            elif method == 'POST':
+                response = requests.post(url, json=data, headers=headers, timeout=10)
+            elif method == 'PATCH':
+                response = requests.patch(url, json=data, headers=headers, timeout=10)
+            else:
+                raise ValueError(f"Unsupported method: {method}")
+
+            success = response.status_code == expected_status
+            details = f"Status: {response.status_code}, Expected: {expected_status}"
+            
+            if not success:
+                try:
+                    error_data = response.json()
+                    details += f", Response: {error_data}"
+                except:
+                    details += f", Response: {response.text[:200]}"
+            
+            self.log_test(name, success, details)
+            
+            return success, response.json() if success and response.content else {}
+
+        except requests.exceptions.Timeout:
+            self.log_test(name, False, "Request timeout (10s)")
+            return False, {}
+        except requests.exceptions.ConnectionError:
+            self.log_test(name, False, "Connection error")
+            return False, {}
+        except Exception as e:
+            self.log_test(name, False, f"Error: {str(e)}")
+            return False, {}
+

 ## Basic Usage ```python from emergentintegrations.llm.chat import LlmChat, UserMessage # Initialize the chat with your API key, session ID, and system message chat = LlmChat( api_key="your-api-key", session_id="unique-session-id", system_message="You are a helpful assistant." ) # Create a simple user message user_message = UserMessage( text="Say 'Hello, integration test!' and nothing else." ) # Send the message and get the response response = await chat.send_message(user_message) print(response) ``` ## Configuration Options The `LlmChat` class provides several configuration methods: ```python # Change the model and provider (default is "gpt-4o" with "openai") chat.with_model("openai", "gpt-4o") # Use Anthropic's Claude chat.with_model("anthropic", "claude-3-7-sonnet-20250219") # Use Gemini chat.with_model("gemini", "gemini-2.0-flash") ## Message Types ### Text Messages ```python user_message = UserMessage( text="Your message here" ) ``` Example: ### Basic Chat with Different Providers ```python # Using OpenAI openai_chat = LlmChat( api_key="your-openai-key", session_id="openai-chat", system_message="You are a helpful assistant." ).with_model("openai", "gpt-4o") # Using Anthropic claude_chat = LlmChat( api_key="your-anthropic-key", session_id="claude-chat", system_message="You are Claude, a helpful AI assistant." ).with_model("anthropic", "claude-3-7-sonnet-20250219") # Using Gemini gemini_chat = LlmChat( api_key="your-gemini-key", session_id="gemini-chat", system_message="You are a helpful assistant." ).with_model("gemini", "gemini-2.0-flash") ``` </setup> <important_pointers> Important pointers: 1. 32|class Bitrix24Service:
33|    def __init__(self):
34|        self.webhook_url = os.getenv("BITRIX24_WEBHOOK_URL", "").rstrip('/')
35|        
36|    async def _make_request(self, method: str, params: Dict = None):
37|        """–ó–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å –∫ Bitrix24 API"""
38|        try:
39|            url = f"{self.webhook_url}/{method}"
40|            async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
41|                async with session.post(url, json=params or {}, timeout=30) as response:
42|                    if response.status == 200:
43|                        return await response.json()
44|                    else:
45|                        error_text = await response.text()
46|                        logger.error(f"Bitrix24 error {response.status}: {error_text}")
47|                        return {"error": f"HTTP {response.status}"}
48|        except Exception as e:
49|            logger.error(f"Bitrix24 request error: {str(e)}")
50|            return {"error": str(e)}
51|    
52|    async def get_deals(self, limit: int = 50):
53|        """–ü–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Å–¥–µ–ª–æ–∫"""
54|        params = {
55|            "SELECT": ["ID", "TITLE", "STAGE_ID", "OPPORTUNITY", "CONTACT_ID", "DATE_CREATE"],
56|            "start": 0,
57|            "limit": limit
58|        }
59|        result = await self._make_request("crm.deal.list", params)
60|        return result.get("result", [])
61|    
62|    async def create_task(self, task_data: Dict):
63|        """–°–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏–µ –∑–∞–¥–∞—á–∏ –≤ Bitrix24"""
64|        params = {
65|            "fields": {
66|                "TITLE": task_data.get("title", ""),
67|                "DESCRIPTION": task_data.get("description", ""),
68|                "RESPONSIBLE_ID": task_data.get("responsible_id", "1"),
69|                "DEADLINE": task_data.get("deadline", ""),
70|            }
71|        }
72|        return await self._make_request("tasks.task.add", params)

84|class TelegramService:
85|    def __init__(self):
86|        self.bot_token = os.getenv("TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN")
87|        self.api_url = f"https://api.telegram.org/bot{self.bot_token}"
88|        
89|    async def send_message(self, chat_id: str, text: str, reply_markup: Dict = None):
90|        """–û—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∫–∞ —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏—è –≤ Telegram"""
91|        try:
92|            url = f"{self.api_url}/sendMessage"
93|            payload = {
94|                "chat_id": chat_id,
95|                "text": text,
96|                "parse_mode": "HTML"
97|            }
98|            if reply_markup:
99|                payload["reply_markup"] = reply_markup
100|                
101|            async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
102|                async with session.post(url, json=payload, timeout=30) as response:
103|                    result = await response.json()
104|                    return result.get("ok", False)
105|        except Exception as e:
106|            logger.error(f"Telegram send error: {str(e)}")
107|            return False
108|    
109|    async def set_webhook(self):
110|        """–£—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–∫–∞ webhook"""
111|        try:
112|            webhook_url = os.getenv("TELEGRAM_WEBHOOK_URL")
113|            url = f"{self.api_url}/setWebhook"
114|            payload = {"url": webhook_url}
115|            
116|            async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
117|                async with session.post(url, json=payload) as response:
118|                    result = await response.json()
119|                    return result
120|        except Exception as e:
121|            return {"ok": False, "error": str(e)}

488|@api_router.post("/meetings/{meeting_id}/analyze")
489|async def analyze_meeting(meeting_id: str):
490|    """AI –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑ –ø–ª–∞–Ω–µ—Ä–∫–∏ –∏ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏–µ –∑–∞–¥–∞—á"""
491|    try:
492|        meeting = await db.meetings.find_one({"id": meeting_id})
493|        if not meeting:
494|            return {"status": "error", "error": "Meeting not found"}
495|        
496|        # AI –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑ –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å–∏ –ø–ª–∞–Ω–µ—Ä–∫–∏
497|        if meeting.get("recording_text"):
498|            analysis_prompt = f"""
499|            –ü—Ä–æ–∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑–∏—Ä—É–π –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å—å –ø–ª–∞–Ω–µ—Ä–∫–∏ –∏ –≤—ã–¥–µ–ª–∏:
500|            1. –ö–ª—é—á–µ–≤—ã–µ —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏—è
501|            2. –ü–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –∑–∞–¥–∞—á–∏
502|            3. –û—Ç–≤–µ—Ç—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö
503|            4. –î–µ–¥–ª–∞–π–Ω—ã
504|            
505|            –ó–∞–ø–∏—Å—å –ø–ª–∞–Ω–µ—Ä–∫–∏:
506|            {meeting['recording_text']}
507|            
508|            –í–µ—Ä–Ω–∏ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç –≤ —Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç–µ JSON:
509|            {
510|                "summary": "–ö—Ä–∞—Ç–∫–æ–µ —Ä–µ–∑—é–º–µ",
511|                "decisions": ["—Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ1", "—Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ2"],
512|                "tasks": [
513|                    {"title": "–ó–∞–¥–∞—á–∞", "responsible": "–§–ò–û", "deadline": "–¥–∞—Ç–∞", "description": "–æ–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–∏–µ"}
514|                ]
515|            }
516|            """
517|

531|                if "tasks" in ai_response.lower():
532|                    # –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º –∑–∞–¥–∞—á–∏ –≤ Bitrix24
533|                    task_result = await bitrix_service.create_task({

560|@api_router.get("/logs")
561|async def get_system_logs(limit: int = 100, level: Optional[str] = None, component: Optional[str] = None):
562|    """–ü–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–Ω—ã—Ö –ª–æ–≥–æ–≤"""

565|        if level:
566|            filter_dict["level"] = level
567|        if component:
568|            filter_dict["component"] = component
569|            
570|        logs = await db.system_logs.find(
571|            filter_dict, 
572|            sort=[("timestamp", -1)]
573|        ).limit(limit).to_list(length=None)
574|        
575|        # –ö–æ–Ω–≤–µ—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä—É–µ–º ObjectId –≤ —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫–∏ –¥–ª—è JSON —Å–µ—Ä–∏–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏
576|        for log in logs:
577|            if "_id" in log:
578|                log["_id"] = str(log["_id"])
579|        
580|        return {"status": "success", "logs": logs, "count": len(logs)}
581|    except Exception as e:
582|        logger.error(f"Get logs error: {str(e)}")
583|        return {"status": "error", "error": str(e)}
584|
585|async def log_system_event(level: str, message: str, component: str, data: Dict = None):
586|    """–§—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏—è –ª–æ–≥–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–Ω—ã—Ö —Å–æ–±—ã—Ç–∏–π"""
587|    try:
588|        log_entry = SystemLog(
589|            level=level,
590|            message=message,
591|            component=component,
592|            data=data or {}
593|        )
594|        await db.system_logs.insert_one(log_entry.dict())
595|        
596|        # –¢–∞–∫–∂–µ –ª–æ–≥–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –≤ Python logger
597|        if level == "ERROR":
598|            logger.error(f"[{component}] {message}")
599|        elif level == "WARNING":
600|            logger.warning(f"[{component}] {message}")
601|        else:
602|            logger.info(f"[{component}] {message}")
603|            
604|    except Exception as e:
605|        logger.error(f"Failed to log system event: {str(e)}")
606|
607|# ============= TELEGRAM BOT ENDPOINTS =============
608|
609|@app.post("/telegram/webhook")
610|async def telegram_webhook(request: Request):
611|    """Webhook –¥–ª—è Telegram –±–æ—Ç–∞"""
612|    try:
613|        data = await request.json()
614|        await log_system_event("INFO", "–ü–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω webhook –æ—Ç Telegram", "telegram", {"update_id": data.get("update_id")})
615|        
616|        if "message" in data:
617|            message = data["message"]
618|            chat_id = str(message["chat"]["id"])
619|            text = message.get("text", "")
620|            user_id = str(message["from"]["id"])
621|            username = message["from"].get("username", "Unknown")
622|            
623|            # –°–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω—è–µ–º —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ
624|            chat_msg = ChatMessage(
625|                sender_id=user_id,

from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse

# ============= MODELS =============

class StatusCheck(BaseModel):
    id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))
    client_name: str
    timestamp: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)

class StatusCheckCreate(BaseModel):
    client_name: str

class Employee(BaseModel):
    id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))
    full_name: str
    phone: str
    role: str
    department: str
    telegram_id: Optional[str] = None
    bitrix24_id: Optional[str] = None
    active: bool = True
    performance_score: float = 0.0
    created_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)

class EmployeeCreate(BaseModel):
    full_name: str
    phone: str
    role: str
    department: str

class ChatMessage(BaseModel):
    id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))
    sender_id: str
    content: str
    ai_response: Optional[str] = None
    timestamp: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)
    chat_type: str = "dashboard"

class Meeting(BaseModel):
    id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))
    title: str
    description: str
    participants: List[str] = []
    start_time: datetime
    recording_text: Optional[str] = None
    ai_summary: Optional[str] = None
    action_items: List[str] = []
    bitrix_tasks_created: List[str] = []
    created_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)

class SystemLog(BaseModel):
    id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))
    level: str
    message: str
    component: str
    data: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
    timestamp: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)

class VoiceCall(BaseModel):
    id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))
    caller_id: str
    duration: int = 0
    transcript: Optional[str] = None
    ai_response_text: Optional[str] = None
    status: str = "active"
    created_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)

class AITask(BaseModel):
    id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))
    title: str
    description: str
    schedule: str
    recurring: bool = True
    next_run: Optional[datetime] = None
    last_run: Optional[datetime] = None
    active: bool = True
    created_by: str
    created_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)

class TrainingFile(BaseModel):

# ============= SERVICES =============

class Bitrix24Service:
    def __init__(self):
        self.webhook_url = os.getenv("BITRIX24_WEBHOOK_URL", "").rstrip('/')
        
    async def _make_request(self, method: str, params: Dict = None):
        try:
            url = f"{self.webhook_url}/{method}"
            async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
                async with session.post(url, json=params or {}, timeout=30) as response:
                    if response.status == 200:
                        return await response.json()
                    else:
                        return {"error": f"HTTP {response.status}"}
        except Exception as e:
            return {"error": str(e)}
    
    async def get_deals(self, limit: int = 50):
        params = {
            "SELECT": ["ID", "TITLE", "STAGE_ID", "OPPORTUNITY", "CONTACT_ID", "DATE_CREATE"],
            "start": 0,
            "limit": limit
        }
        result = await self._make_request("crm.deal.list", params)
        return result.get("result", [])
    
    async def create_task(self, task_data: Dict):
        params = {
            "fields": {
                "TITLE": task_data.get("title", ""),
                "DESCRIPTION": task_data.get("description", ""),
                "RESPONSIBLE_ID": task_data.get("responsible_id", "1"),
                "DEADLINE": task_data.get("deadline", ""),
            }
        }
        return await self._make_request("tasks.task.add", params)

class TelegramService:
    def __init__(self):
        self.bot_token = os.getenv("TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN")
        self.api_url = f"https://api.telegram.org/bot{self.bot_token}"
        
    async def send_message(self, chat_id: str, text: str, reply_markup: Dict = None):
        try:
            url = f"{self.api_url}/sendMessage"
            payload = {"chat_id": chat_id, "text": text, "parse_mode": "HTML"}
            if reply_markup:
                payload["reply_markup"] = reply_markup
                
            async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
                async with session.post(url, json=payload, timeout=30) as response:
                    result = await response.json()
                    return result.get("ok", False)
        except Exception as e:
            return False
    
    async def set_webhook(self):
        try:
            webhook_url = os.getenv("TELEGRAM_WEBHOOK_URL")
            url = f"{self.api_url}/setWebhook"
            payload = {"url": webhook_url}
            
            async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
                async with session.post(url, json=payload) as response:
                    return await response.json()
        except Exception as e:
            return {"ok": False, "error": str(e)}

# Initialize services
bitrix_service = Bitrix24Service()
telegram_service = TelegramService()

# ============= AI SERVICE =============

async def get_ai_response(message: str, context: str = "") -> str:
    try:
        openai_key = os.getenv("OPENROUTER_API_KEY") or os.getenv("EMERGENT_LLM_KEY")
        if not openai_key:
            return f"ü§ñ –°–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–æ: '{message}'. AI —Å–µ—Ä–≤–∏—Å –Ω–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–∞–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è..."
        
        url = "https://api.openai.com/v1/chat/completions"
        if openai_key.startswith("sk-or-"):
            url = "https://openrouter.ai/api/v1/chat/completions"
        elif openai_key.startswith("sk-emergent-"):
            url = "https://emergentmethods.ai/v1/chat/completions"
        
        headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {openai_key}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}
        
        data = {
            "model": "gpt-4o-mini",
            "messages": [
                {
                    "role": "system", 
                    "content": f"""–¢—ã AI-–∞—Å—Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç –∫–æ–º–ø–∞–Ω–∏–∏ –í–∞—Å–î–æ–º - –ª–∏–¥–µ—Ä–∞ –≤ —É–±–æ—Ä–∫–µ –ø–æ–¥—ä–µ–∑–¥–æ–≤ –∏ —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å—Ç–≤–µ –≤ –ö–∞–ª—É–≥–µ.

–ö–û–ù–¢–ï–ö–°–¢: {context}

–ö–û–ú–ü–ê–ù–ò–Ø –í–ê–°–î–û–ú:
- –£–±–æ—Ä–∫–∞ –ø–æ–¥—ä–µ–∑–¥–æ–≤ –≤ 400+ –¥–æ–º–∞—Ö –ö–∞–ª—É–≥–∏
- –°—Ç—Ä–æ–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—ã
- 13+ —Å–æ—Ç—Ä—É–¥–Ω–∏–∫–æ–≤ –≤ –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥–µ
- Bitrix24 CRM –∏–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è

–û—Ç–≤–µ—á–∞–π –ø—Ä–æ—Ñ–µ—Å—Å–∏–æ–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ, –∫—Ä–∞—Ç–∫–æ –∏ –ø–æ –¥–µ–ª—É –Ω–∞ —Ä—É—Å—Å–∫–æ–º —è–∑—ã–∫–µ."""
                },
                {"role": "user", "content": message}
            ],
            "temperature": 0.7,
            "max_tokens": 500
        }
        
        async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
            async with session.post(url, headers=headers, json=data, timeout=30) as response:
                if response.status == 200:
                    result = await response.json()
                    return result["choices"][0]["message"]["content"]
                else:
                    return f"ü§ñ AI –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –Ω–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–µ–Ω. –í–∞—à–µ —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ: '{message}'"
                    
    except Exception as e:
        return f"ü§ñ –°–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ –æ–±—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–Ω–æ: '{message}'. AI –æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç –±—É–¥–µ—Ç –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–µ–Ω –ø–æ–∑–∂–µ."

async def log_system_event(level: str, message: str, component: str, data: Dict = None):
    try:
        log_entry = SystemLog(level=level, message=message, component=component, data=data or {})
        await db.system_logs.insert_one(log_entry.dict())
        
        if level == "ERROR":
            logger.error(f"[{component}] {message}")
        elif level == "WARNING":
            logger.warning(f"[{component}] {message}")
        else:
            logger.info(f"[{component}] {message}")
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Failed to log: {str(e)}")

# ============= BASIC ENDPOINTS =============

@api_router.get("/")
async def root():
    return {"message": "VasDom AudioBot API", "version": "2.0.0", "status": "üöÄ –í—Å–µ –∏–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã"}

@api_router.post("/status", response_model=StatusCheck)
async def create_status_check(input: StatusCheckCreate):
    status_obj = StatusCheck(**input.dict())
    await db.status_checks.insert_one(status_obj.dict())
    return status_obj

@api_router.get("/status", response_model=List[StatusCheck])
async def get_status_checks():
    status_checks = await db.status_checks.find().to_list(1000)
    return [StatusCheck(**status_check) for status_check in status_checks]

# ============= DASHBOARD =============

@api_router.get("/dashboard")
async def get_dashboard():
    try:
        total_employees = await db.employees.count_documents({"active": True})
        total_meetings = await db.meetings.count_documents({})
        total_messages = await db.chat_messages.count_documents({})
        total_voice_calls = await db.voice_calls.count_documents({})
        total_ai_tasks = await db.ai_tasks.count_documents({"active": True})
        total_training_files = await db.training_files.count_documents({})
        
        recent_logs = await db.system_logs.find(
            {"level": {"$in": ["WARNING", "ERROR"]}}, 
            sort=[("timestamp", -1)]
        ).limit(5).to_list(length=None)
        
        return {
            "total_employees": total_employees,
            "total_meetings": total_meetings,
            "total_messages": total_messages,
            "total_voice_calls": total_voice_calls,
            "total_ai_tasks": total_ai_tasks,
            "total_training_files": total_training_files,
            "system_health": "excellent",
            "recent_alerts": len(recent_logs)
        }
    except Exception as e:
        await log_system_event("ERROR", "Dashboard error", "backend", {"error": str(e)})
        return {"error": str(e)}

@api_router.post("/voice/process-audio")
async def process_voice_audio(audio_data: Dict[str, Any]):
    try:
        call_id = audio_data.get("call_id")
        # –ó–∞–≥–ª—É—à–∫–∞ –¥–ª—è —Ä–µ—á–∏ (–≤ production - WebRTC + Speech-to-Text)
        transcript = audio_data.get("transcript", "–ì–æ–ª–æ—Å–æ–≤–æ–µ —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ (—Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏—è –≤ —Ä–∞–∑—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∫–µ)")
        
        ai_response = await get_ai_response(transcript, "–ì–æ–ª–æ—Å–æ–≤–æ–π –∑–≤–æ–Ω–æ–∫ —Å –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª–µ–º")
        
        await db.voice_calls.update_one(
            {"id": call_id},
            {"$set": {"transcript": transcript, "ai_response_text": ai_response}}
        )
        
        return {
            "status": "success",
            "transcript": transcript,
            "ai_response": ai_response,
            "speech_url": "/voice/tts"  # Text-to-Speech URL
        }
    except Exception as e:
        return {"status": "error", "error": str(e)}

@api_router.post("/meetings/start-recording")
async def start_meeting_recording(meeting_data: Dict[str, Any]):

            participants=meeting_data.get("participants", []),
            start_time=datetime.utcnow()
        )
        
        await db.meetings.insert_one(meeting.dict())
        await log_system_event("INFO", f"üé§ –ù–∞—á–∞—Ç–∞ –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å—å –ø–ª–∞–Ω–µ—Ä–∫–∏: {meeting.title}", "meetings")
        
        return {"status": "success", "meeting_id": meeting.id, "message": "üé§ –î–∏–∫—Ç–æ—Ñ–æ–Ω –≤–∫–ª—é—á–µ–Ω"}
    except Exception as e:
        return {"status": "error", "error": str(e)}

@api_router.post("/meetings/{meeting_id}/add-transcript")

        await db.meetings.update_one({"id": meeting_id}, {"$set": {"recording_text": transcript}})
        await log_system_event("INFO", f"üìù –î–æ–±–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—Å–∫—Ä–∏–ø—Ç: {meeting_id}", "meetings")

    except Exception as e:
        return {"status": "error", "error": str(e)}

@api_router.get("/meetings")
async def get_meetings(limit: int = 20):
    try:
        meetings = await db.meetings.find({}, sort=[("start_time", -1)]).limit(limit).to_list(length=None)
        for meeting in meetings:
            if "_id" in meeting:
                meeting["_id"] = str(meeting["_id"])
        return {"status": "success", "meetings": meetings}
    except Exception as e:
        return {"status": "error", "error": str(e)}

@api_router.post("/meetings/{meeting_id}/analyze")
async def analyze_meeting(meeting_id: str):
    try:
        meeting = await db.meetings.find_one({"id": meeting_id})
        if not meeting or not meeting.get("recording_text"):
            return {"status": "error", "error": "–ù–µ—Ç –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å–∏ –¥–ª—è –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞"}
        
        analysis_prompt = f"""–ü—Ä–æ–∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑–∏—Ä—É–π –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å—å –ø–ª–∞–Ω–µ—Ä–∫–∏ –í–∞—Å–î–æ–º –∏ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–π:
1. –ö—Ä–∞—Ç–∫–æ–µ —Ä–µ–∑—é–º–µ (2-3 –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è)
2. –°–ø–∏—Å–æ–∫ –∫–æ–Ω–∫—Ä–µ—Ç–Ω—ã—Ö –∑–∞–¥–∞—á —Å –æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–º–∏
3. –î–µ–¥–ª–∞–π–Ω—ã

–ó–∞–ø–∏—Å—å: {meeting['recording_text']}

–û—Ç–≤–µ—Ç—å —á–µ—Ç–∫–æ —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–æ."""

        ai_analysis = await get_ai_response(analysis_prompt, "–ê–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑ –ø–ª–∞–Ω–µ—Ä–∫–∏ –í–∞—Å–î–æ–º")
        
        await db.meetings.update_one(
            {"id": meeting_id}, 
            {"$set": {"ai_summary": ai_analysis, "analyzed_at": datetime.utcnow()}}
        )
        
        # –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º –∑–∞–¥–∞—á–∏ –≤ Bitrix24
        bitrix_tasks = []
        try:
            task_result = await bitrix_service.create_task({
                "title": f"–ó–∞–¥–∞—á–∏ —Å –ø–ª–∞–Ω–µ—Ä–∫–∏: {meeting['title']}",
                "description": ai_analysis,
                "responsible_id": "1"
            })
            if task_result.get("result"):
                bitrix_tasks.append(task_result["result"])
                await log_system_event("INFO", f"üéØ –ó–∞–¥–∞—á–∞ –≤ Bitrix24: {task_result['result']}", "bitrix24")
        except Exception:
            pass
        
        return {"status": "success", "analysis": ai_analysis, "bitrix_tasks": bitrix_tasks}
    except Exception as e:
        return {"status": "error", "error": str(e)}

# ============= CLEANING HOUSES (–†–ê–ë–û–¢–´ - –ö–õ–ò–ù–ò–ù–ì) =============

@api_router.get("/cleaning/houses")
async def get_cleaning_houses():
    try:
        deals = await bitrix_service.get_deals(limit=500)
        houses = []
        
        for deal in deals:
            house = CleaningHouse(
                address=deal.get("TITLE", ""),
                stage=deal.get("STAGE_ID", ""),
                bitrix24_deal_id=deal["ID"],
                contact_info=deal.get("CONTACT_ID", "")
            )
            houses.append(house.dict())
        
        # –°–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–∏–∑–∏—Ä—É–µ–º —Å –ª–æ–∫–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–π –±–∞–∑–æ–π
        for house_data in houses:
            existing = await db.cleaning_houses.find_one({"bitrix24_deal_id": house_data["bitrix24_deal_id"]})
            if not existing:
                await db.cleaning_houses.insert_one(house_data)
        
        await log_system_event("INFO", f"üè† –°–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–∏–∑–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–æ {len(houses)} –¥–æ–º–æ–≤", "cleaning")
        return {"status": "success", "houses": houses, "total": len(houses)}
    except Exception as e:
        return {"status": "error", "error": str(e)}

# ============= AI TASKS (–ó–ê–î–ê–ß–ò –î–õ–Ø AI) =============

@api_router.post("/ai-tasks")
async def create_ai_task(task_data: Dict[str, Any]):
    try:
        ai_task = AITask(
            title=task_data["title"],
            description=task_data["description"],
            schedule=task_data.get("schedule", ""),
            recurring=task_data.get("recurring", False),
            created_by=task_data.get("created_by", "admin")
        )
        
        # –í—ã—á–∏—Å–ª—è–µ–º —Å–ª–µ–¥—É—é—â–∏–π –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫
        if ai_task.recurring and "–µ–∂–µ–¥–Ω–µ–≤–Ω–æ" in ai_task.schedule.lower():
            ai_task.next_run = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(days=1)
        elif ai_task.recurring and "–µ–∂–µ–Ω–µ–¥–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ" in ai_task.schedule.lower():
            ai_task.next_run = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(days=7)
        
        await db.ai_tasks.insert_one(ai_task.dict())
        await log_system_event("INFO", f"ü§ñ –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∞ AI –∑–∞–¥–∞—á–∞: {ai_task.title}", "ai_tasks")
        
        return {"status": "success", "task": ai_task.dict()}
    except Exception as e:
        return {"status": "error", "error": str(e)}

        return {"status": "error", "error": str(e)}

        ).limit(limit).to_list(length=None)

        return {"status": "success", "messages": messages[::-1]}
    except Exception as e:
        return {"status": "error", "error": str(e)}

# ============= TELEGRAM BOT =============

@app.post("/telegram/webhook")
async def telegram_webhook(request: Request):
    try:
        data = await request.json()
        await log_system_event("INFO", "üì± Telegram webhook –ø–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω", "telegram", {"update_id": data.get("update_id")})
        
        if "message" in data:
            message = data["message"]
            chat_id = str(message["chat"]["id"])
            text = message.get("text", "")
            user_id = str(message["from"]["id"])
            username = message["from"].get("username", "Unknown")
            
            chat_msg = ChatMessage(sender_id=user_id, content=text, chat_type="telegram")
            await db.chat_messages.insert_one(chat_msg.dict())
            
            if text.startswith("/start"):
                employee = await db.employees.find_one({"telegram_id": user_id})
                
                if employee:
                    welcome_text = f"üëã –ü—Ä–∏–≤–µ—Ç, {employee['full_name']}!\n\nü§ñ VasDom AudioBot –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤!\n\nüìã /tasks - –∑–∞–¥–∞—á–∏\n‚ùì /help - –ø–æ–º–æ—â—å"
                else:
                    welcome_text = "üëã –î–æ–±—Ä–æ –ø–æ–∂–∞–ª–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –≤ VasDom AudioBot!\n\nüîç –ü–æ–∂–∞–ª—É–π—Å—Ç–∞, –∑–∞—Ä–µ–≥–∏—Å—Ç—Ä–∏—Ä—É–π—Ç–µ—Å—å –≤ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–µ.\n\nüìû –ê–¥–º–∏–Ω–∏—Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä:\n‚Ä¢ –ú–∞–∫—Å–∏–º: +7 920 092 4550"
                
                await telegram_service.send_message(chat_id, welcome_text)
                
            elif text.startswith("/help"):
                help_text = """ü§ñ <b>VasDom AudioBot</b>

üìã <b>–ö–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥—ã:</b>
‚Ä¢ /start - –Ω–∞—á–∞—Ç—å —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—É
‚Ä¢ /tasks - –º–æ–∏ –∑–∞–¥–∞—á–∏
‚Ä¢ /help - —Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∫–∞

üè¢ <b>–í–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏:</b>
‚Ä¢ AI-–∞—Å—Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç 24/7
‚Ä¢ –ò–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è —Å Bitrix24
‚Ä¢ –ü–ª–∞–Ω–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç
‚Ä¢ –û—Ç—á–µ—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å

üìû <b>–ü–æ–¥–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∫–∞:</b>
‚Ä¢ +7 920 092 4550 (–ú–∞–∫—Å–∏–º)"""

                await telegram_service.send_message(chat_id, help_text)
                
            else:
                # AI –æ–±—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∫–∞
                ai_response = await get_ai_response(text, f"Telegram: {username}")
                await db.chat_messages.update_one({"id": chat_msg.id}, {"$set": {"ai_response": ai_response}})
                await telegram_service.send_message(chat_id, f"ü§ñ {ai_response}")
                await log_system_event("INFO", "ü§ñ AI –æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç –≤ Telegram", "telegram", {"user": username})
        
        return {"status": "ok"}
    except Exception as e:
        await log_system_event("ERROR", "Telegram error", "telegram", {"error": str(e)})
        return {"status": "error", "message": str(e)}

@app.get("/telegram/set-webhook")
async def set_telegram_webhook():
    try:
        result = await telegram_service.set_webhook()
        await log_system_event("INFO", "üì± Telegram webhook —É—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω", "telegram", result)
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        return {"error": str(e)}
